```python
data['Size']=data.Size.replace("Varies with device",np.nan)
data['Size']=data.Size.str.replace("M","000")
data['Size']=data.Size.str.replace("k","")
data['Size']=data.Size.replace("1,000+",1000)
data['Size']=data['Size'].astype(float)
data['Size'].dtype
```

```python
def add_age(cols):
    Age=cols[0];
    Pclass=cols[1];
    if pd.isnull(Age):
        return int(df[df["Pclass"]==Pclass]["Age"].mean())
    else:
        return Age
```


```python
df["Age"]=df[["Age","Pclass"]].apply(add_age,axis=1)
```

```python
sex=pd.get_dummies(df["Sex"],drop_first=True)
```


```python
embarked=pd.get_dummies(df["Embarked"],drop_first=True)
pclass=pd.get_dummies(df["Pclass"],drop_first=True)
```


```python
df=pd.concat([df,pclass,sex,embarked],axis=1)
```

```python
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
X_train, X_test, Y_train, Y_test=train_test_split(X,Y,test_size=0.25,random_state=101)
```


```python
from sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression
logmodel=LogisticRegression(random_state=101)
logmodel.fit(X_train,Y_train)
```
